<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b>Item 5.07 Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">At the 2020 Annual Meeting of Shareholders of the Company held
on May&#160;12, 2020, the votes cast with respect to each item of business properly presented at the meeting are as follows:</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Proposal No.&#160;1 &#8212; The shareholders elected each of
the eleven nominees to the Board of Directors for a one-year term by the vote of the majority of votes cast, in accordance with
3M&#8217;s Bylaws.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0.75in 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">*Under the General Corporation Law of the State of
Delaware, the affirmative &#8220;FOR&#8221; vote of a majority of those shares present in person or represented by proxy at
the meeting and entitled to vote on the matter is required to approve the shareholder proposal. In tabulating the voting
result, abstentions and, if applicable, broker non-votes are not counted as votes &#8220;FOR&#8221; or &#8220;AGAINST&#8221;
the proposal. An abstention will, however, be counted as entitled to vote on a proposal and will, therefore, have the effect
of a vote &#8220;AGAINST.&#8221;&#160; Applying this standard, the percentage in favor of the shareholder proposal is
calculated by dividing the number of FOR votes by the sum of the number of FOR, AGAINST and ABSTAIN votes.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></p>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2 -->
    <div style="border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><p style="margin: 0pt">&#160;</p></div>
    <div style="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><p style="margin: 0pt">&#160;</p></div>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; text-indent: 0in">SIGNATURE</p>
